004796: const renderProgressive = (tbody, data, renderRowFn, chunkSize = 40) => {
004797:   const token=(APP_RUNTIME.renderTokens.get(tbody)||0)+1;APP_RUNTIME.renderTokens.set(tbody,token);
004798:   tbody.innerHTML = "";
004799:   if (!data || !data.length) return;
004800:   const safeChunkSize = data.length > 5000 ? Math.min(chunkSize, 28) : chunkSize;
004801:   let index = 0;
004802:   const renderNextChunk = () => {
004803:       if(APP_RUNTIME.renderTokens.get(tbody)!==token)return;
004804:       const chunk = data.slice(index, index + safeChunkSize);
004805:       if (!chunk.length) return;
004806:       const fragment = document.createDocumentFragment();
004807:       const temp = document.createElement("tbody");
004808:       temp.innerHTML = chunk.map(renderRowFn).join("");
004809:       while(temp.firstChild) fragment.appendChild(temp.firstChild);
004810:       if(APP_RUNTIME.renderTokens.get(tbody)!==token)return;
004811:       tbody.appendChild(fragment);
004812:       index += safeChunkSize;
004813:       if (index < data.length) scheduleUiWork(renderNextChunk);
004814:   };
004815:   // Render the first chunk immediately so a filter change never leaves the table visually blank.
004816:   // Remaining chunks still use idle/animation scheduling to keep large datasets responsive.
004817:   renderNextChunk();
004818: };

004820: const fmtMoney = (v) => isFinite(v) ? new Intl.NumberFormat("en-US",{maximumFractionDigits:2}).format(v) : "0.00"; 
004821: const fmtInt = (v) => new Intl.NumberFormat("en-US",{maximumFractionDigits:0}).format(v||0);
004822: const fmtPct = (v) => { 
004823:   if (v === null || v === undefined) return "N/A";
004824:   if (v === Infinity) return "∞";
004825:   if (!isFinite(v)) return "N/A"; 
004826:   if (v < 0) return "-" + Math.abs(v*100).toFixed(2) + "%"; 
004827:   return (v*100).toFixed(2)+"%"; 
004828: }
004829: 
004830: // One global visual rule for actual ACOS values across every module.
004831: // 1%-39% = green; 40%-60% = yellow; >=61% (and Infinity) = red.

004916: const parsePercent = (x) => {
004917:   if (typeof x === "number") {
004918:     if (!isFinite(x)) return 0;
004919:     return Math.abs(x) > 1 ? x / 100 : x;
004920:   }
004921:   if (x === null || x === undefined || x === "") return 0;
004922:   const raw = String(x).trim();
004923:   const n = safeNum(raw);
004924:   if (!isFinite(n)) return 0;
004925:   return raw.includes("%") || Math.abs(n) > 1 ? n / 100 : n;
004926: };

004928: const parsePercentField = (x, field="generic", source="") => {
004929:   if(x===null||x===undefined||x==="")return {value:0,ambiguous:false};
004930:   const raw=String(x).trim(),n=safeNum(raw);if(!Number.isFinite(n))return {value:0,ambiguous:false};
004931:   const hasPct=raw.includes("%");if(hasPct)return {value:n/100,ambiguous:false};
004932:   const ratioFields=new Set(["ctr","cvr","acos","share","rate"]),adjustFields=new Set(["placementAdjustment"]);
004933:   if(adjustFields.has(field))return {value:Math.abs(n)>10?n/100:(Math.abs(n)>1?n/100:n),ambiguous:Math.abs(n)===1};
004934:   if(ratioFields.has(field)){
004935:     if(Math.abs(n)<1)return {value:n,ambiguous:false};
004936:     if(Math.abs(n)>1)return {value:n/100,ambiguous:false};
004937:     const warning={fileName:source||"",reportType:"PERCENT_FIELD",warning:`Ambiguous naked percent value 1 in ${field}`};AdsStore.importWarnings.push(warning);return {value:n/100,ambiguous:true};
004938:   }
004939:   return {value:Math.abs(n)>1?n/100:n,ambiguous:Math.abs(n)===1};
004940: };

005092: 
005093: const levenshtein = (a, b) => {
005094:     if (a === b) return 0;
005095:     if (a.length > b.length) { let tmp = a; a = b; b = tmp; }
005096:     let al = a.length, bl = b.length;
005097:     if (al === 0) return bl;
005098:     let row = Array.from({length: al + 1}, (_, i) => i);
005099:     let res = 0;
005100:     for (let i = 1; i <= bl; i++) {
005101:         res = i;
005102:         let diag = i - 1;
005103:         for (let j = 1; j <= al; j++) {
005104:             let cost = a[j - 1] === b[i - 1] ? 0 : 1;
005105:             let nextDiag = row[j];
005106:             res = Math.min(res + 1, nextDiag + 1, diag + cost);
005107:             row[j - 1] = diag;
005108:             diag = nextDiag;
005109:         }
005110:         row[al] = res;
005111:     }
005112:     return res;
005113: };

005519: const normalizeAdProductValue = (value) => {
005520:     const v = String(value || "").trim().toLowerCase();
005521:     if (!v) return "";
005522:     if (v.includes("sponsored display") || v === "sd" || v.includes("display ads") || v.includes("display")) return "SD";
005523:     if (v.includes("sponsored brand") || v === "sb" || v.includes("brand")) return "SB";
005524:     if (v.includes("sponsored product") || v === "sp" || v.includes("product")) return "SP";
005525:     return "";
005526: };

005528: const detectAdProduct = (headers, sampleRows = [], adProductCol = null) => {
005529:     if (adProductCol && sampleRows.length) {
005530:       for (const row of sampleRows.slice(0, 80)) {
005531:         const detected = normalizeAdProductValue(row?.[adProductCol]);
005532:         if (detected) return detected;
005533:       }
005534:     }
005535:     const joined = headers.map(cleanHeader).join("|");
005536:     if (joined.includes("viewableimpression") || joined.includes("vpm") || joined.includes("view-through") || joined.includes("viewthrough") || joined.includes("display")) return "SD";
005537:     if (joined.includes("ntb") || joined.includes("new-to-brand") || joined.includes("newtobrand") || joined.includes("brandimpression")) return "SB";
005538:     return "SP"; 
005539: };

005825: const repairWorksheetRange = (ws) => {
005826:   if (!ws) return ws;
005827:   let maxR = -1, maxC = -1;
005828:   const dense = Array.isArray(ws) ? ws : (Array.isArray(ws["!data"]) ? ws["!data"] : null);

005830:     for (let r = 0; r < dense.length; r++) {
005831:       const row = dense[r]; if (!row) continue;

005833:         if (row[c] !== undefined && row[c] !== null) { maxR = Math.max(maxR, r); maxC = Math.max(maxC, c); break; }
005834:       }
005835:     }
005836:   } else {

005927:     if (!Number.isFinite(r.restOfSearchAdjustment)) r.restOfSearchAdjustment = control.restOfSearchAdjustment;
005928:     if (!r.advertisedAsin) r.advertisedAsin = control.advertisedAsin;
005929:     if (!r.advertisedSku) r.advertisedSku = control.advertisedSku;
005930:   }
005931: };
005932: const resolveAnalysisGrain = (rows = AdsStore.all, requested = "auto") => {
005933:   if (requested && requested !== "auto") return requested;
005934:   const stats=getGrainReconciliation(rows||[]),st=stats.searchTerm,tg=stats.targeting,cp=stats.campaign;
005935:   const score=x=>(x.spendCoverage||0)*.5+Math.min(1,(x.campaigns||0)/Math.max(1,Math.max(st.campaigns,tg.campaigns,cp.campaigns)))*.3+Math.min(1,(x.dates||0)/Math.max(1,Math.max(st.dates,tg.dates,cp.dates)))*.2;
005936:   if(st.rows&&score(st)>=score(tg)*.82)return "searchTerm";
005937:   if(tg.rows)return "targeting";
005938:   if(cp.rows)return "campaign";
005939:   return "searchTerm";
005940: };
005941: const weightedCoverage = (rows, predicate, weightKey = "spend") => {
005942:   let total=0, covered=0;
005943:   for (const r of rows || []) { const w=Math.max(0,safeNum(r[weightKey])) || (weightKey === "spend" ? Math.max(1,safeNum(r.clicks)) : 1); total+=w; if (predicate(r)) covered+=w; }
005944:   return total > 0 ? clamp(covered/total,0,1) : 0;
005945: };
005946: const getPeriodComparison = (rows = []) => {
005947:   const dates=[...new Set(rows.map(r=>r.date).filter(Boolean))].sort();
005948:   if (dates.length < 4) return null;
005949:   const window=Math.min(7,Math.floor(dates.length/2));
005950:   const recentDates=new Set(dates.slice(-window)), priorDates=new Set(dates.slice(-window*2,-window));
005951:   const recent=sumMetrics(rows.filter(r=>recentDates.has(r.date))), prior=sumMetrics(rows.filter(r=>priorDates.has(r.date)));
005952:   const delta=(a,b)=>b>0?(a-b)/b:(a>0?1:null);
005953:   return { window, recent, prior, spend:delta(recent.spend,prior.spend), sales:delta(recent.sales,prior.sales), roas:delta(recent.roas,prior.roas), cpc:delta(recent.cpc,prior.cpc), cvr:delta(recent.cvr,prior.cvr), profit:delta(recent.contributionProfit,prior.contributionProfit) };
005954: };
005955: const getDataQualityAudit = (rows = AdsStore.view || []) => {
005956:   const scope=getExecutiveDateScope(rows),total=sumMetrics(rows),now=new Date();now.setHours(0,0,0,0);const end=scope.end?new Date(scope.end+"T00:00:00"):null,staleDays=end?Math.max(0,Math.floor((now-end)/86400000)):999,dateCoverage=weightedCoverage(rows,r=>!!r.date,"spend"),structureCoverage=weightedCoverage(rows,r=>!!r.campaign&&!!r.adGroup,"spend"),asinCoverage=weightedCoverage(rows,r=>!!r.advertisedAsin,"spend"),bidCoverage=weightedCoverage(rows,r=>Number.isFinite(r.currentBid)&&r.currentBid>0,"spend"),strategyCoverage=weightedCoverage(rows,r=>!!r.biddingStrategy,"spend"),placementControlCoverage=weightedCoverage(rows,r=>Number.isFinite(r.topOfSearchAdjustment)||Number.isFinite(r.productPagesAdjustment)||Number.isFinite(r.restOfSearchAdjustment),"spend"),explicitUnitsCoverage=total.explicitUnitsCoverage??(total.units>0?clamp(total.explicitUnits/total.units,0,1):0),haloKnownCoverage=total.haloKnownCoverage??1,strictEconomicsCoverage=(explicitUnitsCoverage>=.90?0.5:0)+(haloKnownCoverage>=.90?0.5:0),metricAnomalyCount=(rows||[]).filter(r=>safeNum(r.clicks)>safeNum(r.impr)||(safeNum(r.clicks)<=0&&(safeNum(r.spend)>0||safeNum(r.orders)>0||safeNum(r.sales)>0))).length,metricAnomalyRate=(rows||[]).length?metricAnomalyCount/(rows||[]).length:0,econ=parseAsinEconomicsOverrides(),bizResult=getExecutiveBizSales(rows,scope),salesResult=getExecutiveAccountSales(rows,scope),adProducts=[...new 005957:   let sourceHealthScore=Math.round(clamp(dateCoverage*18+(1-Math.min(1,dupRate*5))*18+(1-Math.min(1,quarantineRate))*18+(workspaceMismatch?0:14)+(rawGrains.length?14:0)+(Math.max(recon.searchTerm.spendCoverage||0,recon.targeting.spendCoverage||0)>=.8?18:8)-Math.min(10,metricAnomalyRate*1000),0,100));

005964:   if(!negativeFreshEnough)alerts.push({level:"bad",text:`最新数据距今 ${staleDays} 天，超过否定/结构执行上限 ${negativeStaleLimit} 天；仅保留历史复核。`});else if(!bidFreshEnough)alerts.push({level:"warn",text:`最新数据距今 ${staleDays} 天：安全否定与结构候选可继续复核，但即时调价要求 ≤${bidStaleLimit} 天的新数据。`});

007742: const getBidGovPosterior = (metrics,prior={mean:.05,strength:24}) => {
007743:   const clicks=Math.max(0,safeNum(metrics.clicks)),orders=Math.max(0,Math.min(clicks,safeNum(metrics.orders))),a=orders+prior.mean*prior.strength,b=Math.max(0,clicks-orders)+(1-prior.mean)*prior.strength,mean=a/Math.max(1,a+b),variance=(a*b)/Math.max(1,((a+b)**2)*(a+b+1)),sd=Math.sqrt(Math.max(0,variance)),z=1.645;
007744:   return {mean,lower:clamp(mean-z*sd,0,1),upper:clamp(mean+z*sd,0,1),priorMean:prior.mean,priorStrength:prior.strength};
007745: };

007748:   return clamp(Math.round(clickScore+orderScore+dayScore+spendScore-penalty),0,100);
007749: };

008159: const scoreActionConfidence = (it, actionKey, guard, intent) => {
008160:   let score = 0.50;
008161:   const clicks = safeNum(it.clicks), spend = safeNum(it.spend), orders = safeNum(it.orders), roas = safeNum(it.roas), cvr = safeNum(it.cvr);
008162:   if (clicks >= 50 || orders >= 5) score += 0.22;
008163:   else if (clicks >= 20 || orders >= 2 || spend >= 30) score += 0.14;
008164:   else if (clicks >= 10 || spend >= 12) score += 0.06;
008165: 
008166:   if (actionKey === "negate" && orders === 0 && spend >= (safeNum($("ruleSpendNeg")?.value) || 30)) score += 0.16;
008167:   const profitPolicy=resolveProfitPolicyForMetrics(it,it.advertisedAsin||it.asin||"");
008168:   if (["exact","phrase","broad","increase"].includes(actionKey) && orders >= 2 && profitPolicy.ready && roas >= profitPolicy.targetRoas) score += 0.18;
008169:   if (actionKey === "decrease" && ((orders === 0 && spend >= 10) || (orders > 0 && profitPolicy.ready && roas < profitPolicy.targetRoas))) score += 0.10;
008170:   if (intent?.key === "mismatch" && actionKey === "negate") score += 0.10;
008171:   if (intent?.key === "male" || intent?.key === "brand") score -= 0.25;
008172:   if (guard?.level === "review") score -= 0.18;
008173:   if (guard?.level === "block") score -= 0.35;
008174:   if (orders === 0 && clicks < 8 && spend < 10) score -= 0.12;
008175:   if (cvr > 0 && cvr < 0.02 && clicks >= 20) score += 0.04;
008176:   if ((it.orderDays || 0) >= getMinStableDays()) score += 0.08;
008177:   if ((it.activeDays || 0) >= 7) score += 0.04;
008178:   if (it.cannibalized) score -= 0.10;
008179:   const dq = AdsStore.dataQuality;
008180:   if (dq?.grade === "A") score += 0.06; else if (dq?.grade === "C") score -= 0.08; else if (dq?.grade === "D") score -= 0.18;
008181: 
008182:   score = Math.max(0.05, Math.min(0.98, score));
008183:   const label = score >= 0.78 ? (currentLang === "zh" ? "高" : "High") : score >= 0.58 ? (currentLang === "zh" ? "中" : "Medium") : (currentLang === "zh" ? "低" : "Low");
008184:   const tagClass = score >= 0.78 && guard?.level !== "review" ? "good" : score < 0.58 || guard?.level === "review" || guard?.level === "block" ? "warn" : "good";
008185:   const sample = clicks >= 50 || orders >= 5 ? (currentLang === "zh" ? "样本足" : "Strong sample") : clicks >= 20 || spend >= 20 ? (currentLang === "zh" ? "样本中" : "Medium sample") : (currentLang === "zh" ? "样本低" : "Low sample");
008186:   const risk = guard?.level === "block" ? (currentLang === "zh" ? "禁止自动执行" : "Blocked") : guard?.level === "review" ? (currentLang === "zh" ? "人工复核" : "Human review") : (currentLang === "zh" ? "可执行" : "Executable");
008187:   return { score, label, tagClass, sample, risk };
008188: };

008341: const actionV4Impact=(it,actionKey,activeDays=Math.max(1,it.activeDays||1))=>{

008345:   if(actionKey==="decrease")return {kind:"savings",amount:spend30*.20,label:actionV4Text("预计降低花费","Est. spend reduction")};
008346:   if(actionKey==="increase")return {kind:"sales",amount:sales30*.12,label:actionV4Text("预计销售机会","Est. sales opportunity")};

008515: const validateKeywordTextForBulk = (keyword, matchType = "") => {
008516:   const text = String(keyword || "").trim().replace(/\s+/g, " ");
008517:   if (!text) return { ok:false, issue:"Empty keyword" };
008518:   if (text.length > AMAZON_BULK_LIMITS.KEYWORD_MAX_CHARS) return { ok:false, issue:`Keyword exceeds ${AMAZON_BULK_LIMITS.KEYWORD_MAX_CHARS} chars` };
008519:   const maxWords = String(matchType).toLowerCase() === "negative phrase" ? AMAZON_BULK_LIMITS.NEGATIVE_PHRASE_MAX_WORDS : AMAZON_BULK_LIMITS.KEYWORD_MAX_WORDS;
008520:   if (text.split(/\s+/).length > maxWords) return { ok:false, issue:`${matchType || "Keyword"} exceeds ${maxWords} words` };
008521:   if (/[<>={}\\]/.test(text)) return { ok:false, issue:"Keyword contains invalid bulk characters" };
008522:   return { ok:true, issue:"" };
008523: };

008525: const validateSponsoredProductsBulkDraft = (headers = [], rows = [], sourceLabel = "Bulk Draft") => {
008526:   const idx = Object.fromEntries(headers.map((h, i) => [h, i]));
008527:   const issues = [];
008528:   const adGroupKeywordCount = new Map();
008529:   const campaignNegKeywordCount = new Map();
008530:   const adGroupNegKeywordCount = new Map();
008531:   const adGroupNegProductCount = new Map();
008532:   const addIssue = (severity, rowNo, field, issue, fix = "") => issues.push([severity, rowNo, field, issue, fix, sourceLabel]);
008533:   rows.forEach((row, i) => {
008534:     const rowNo = i + 2;
008535:     const product = String(row[idx.Product] || "").trim();
008536:     const entity = String(row[idx.Entity] || "").trim();
008537:     const campaign = String(row[idx["Campaign Name"]] || "").trim();
008538:     const adGroup = String(row[idx["Ad Group Name"]] || "").trim();
008539:     const keyword = String(row[idx["Keyword Text"]] || "").trim();
008540:     const expression = String(row[idx["Product Targeting Expression"]] || "").trim();
008541:     const matchType = String(row[idx["Match Type"]] || "").trim().toLowerCase();
008542:     const state = String(row[idx.State] || "").trim().toLowerCase();
008543:     const bid = safeNum(row[idx.Bid]);
008544:     if (product !== "Sponsored Products") addIssue("ERROR", rowNo, "Product", "Only Sponsored Products bulk rows are allowed in this draft", "Move SB/Display rows to analysis-only sheet");
008545:     if (!campaign || /\[.*required.*\]|\[.*campaign.*\]/i.test(campaign)) addIssue("ERROR", rowNo, "Campaign Name", "Campaign placeholder or empty campaign", "Confirm exact campaign name before upload");
008546:     const isNegativeKeywordEntity = /negative/i.test(entity) && /keyword/i.test(entity);
008547:     const isCampaignLevelNegativeKeyword = isNegativeKeywordEntity && !adGroup;
008548:     if ((!adGroup && !isCampaignLevelNegativeKeyword) || /\[.*required.*\]|\[.*ad group.*\]/i.test(adGroup)) addIssue("ERROR", rowNo, "Ad Group Name", "Ad group placeholder or empty ad group", "Confirm exact ad group name before upload; campaign-level negative keywords may leave Ad Group blank");
008549:     if (!state) addIssue("ERROR", rowNo, "State", "Missing state", "Use paused before launch review");
008550:     else if (!["enabled", "paused", "archived"].includes(state)) addIssue("ERROR", rowNo, "State", "Invalid state", "Use paused before launch review");
008551:     if (/keyword/i.test(entity)) {
008552:       const v = validateKeywordTextForBulk(keyword, matchType);
008553:       if (!v.ok) addIssue("ERROR", rowNo, "Keyword Text", v.issue, "Edit keyword before upload");
008554:       if (!["exact", "phrase", "broad", "negative exact", "negative phrase"].includes(matchType)) addIssue("ERROR", rowNo, "Match Type", "Invalid keyword match type", "Use exact/phrase/broad/negative exact/negative phrase");
008555:       if (!/negative/i.test(entity) && bid <= 0) addIssue("ERROR", rowNo, "Bid", "Missing or zero bid", "Confirm bid before enabling");
008556:       const agKey = `${campaign}|${adGroup}`;
008557:       if (!/negative/i.test(entity)) adGroupKeywordCount.set(agKey, (adGroupKeywordCount.get(agKey) || 0) + 1);
008558:       else {
008559:         campaignNegKeywordCount.set(campaign, (campaignNegKeywordCount.get(campaign) || 0) + 1);
008560:         if (adGroup) adGroupNegKeywordCount.set(agKey, (adGroupNegKeywordCount.get(agKey) || 0) + 1);
008561:       }
008562:     }
008563:     if (/product targeting/i.test(entity)) {
008564:       const asin = extractAsinFromText(expression);
008565:       if (!asin) addIssue("ERROR", rowNo, "Product Targeting Expression", "Invalid or missing ASIN targeting expression", 'Use asin="B0XXXXXXXX"');
008566:       if (/negative/i.test(entity)) adGroupNegProductCount.set(`${campaign}|${adGroup}`, (adGroupNegProductCount.get(`${campaign}|${adGroup}`) || 0) + 1);
008567:       else if (bid <= 0) addIssue("ERROR", rowNo, "Bid", "Missing or zero product targeting bid", "Confirm bid before enabling");
008568:     }
008569:   });
008570:   for (const [key, count] of adGroupKeywordCount) if (count > AMAZON_BULK_LIMITS.KEYWORDS_PER_MANUAL_AD_GROUP) addIssue("ERROR", "GROUP", key, `Manual ad group keyword count ${count} exceeds ${AMAZON_BULK_LIMITS.KEYWORDS_PER_MANUAL_AD_GROUP}`, "Split into another ad group");
008571:   for (const [key, count] of campaignNegKeywordCount) if (count > AMAZON_BULK_LIMITS.NEGATIVE_KEYWORDS_PER_CAMPAIGN) addIssue("ERROR", "CAMPAIGN", key, `Campaign negative keyword count ${count} exceeds ${AMAZON_BULK_LIMITS.NEGATIVE_KEYWORDS_PER_CAMPAIGN}`, "Prune or split negatives");
008572:   for (const [key, count] of adGroupNegKeywordCount) if (count > AMAZON_BULK_LIMITS.NEGATIVE_KEYWORDS_PER_AD_GROUP) addIssue("ERROR", "ADGROUP", key, `Ad group negative keyword count ${count} exceeds ${AMAZON_BULK_LIMITS.NEGATIVE_KEYWORDS_PER_AD_GROUP}`, "Prune or split negatives");
008573:   for (const [key, count] of adGroupNegProductCount) if (count > AMAZON_BULK_LIMITS.NEGATIVE_PRODUCTS_PER_AD_GROUP) addIssue("ERROR", "ADGROUP", key, `Ad group negative product count ${count} exceeds ${AMAZON_BULK_LIMITS.NEGATIVE_PRODUCTS_PER_AD_GROUP}`, "Prune negative ASINs");
008574:   if (!issues.length) issues.push(["OK", "-", "-", "Bulk draft passed local guardrail checks", "Still review Campaign/Ad Group/Bid in Amazon Bulk Operations", sourceLabel]);
008575:   return issues;
008576: };

009767: const isStudioAutoHandoverEligible = (row, rules = {}) => {

009773:

009775:   const autoClicks = safeNum(row?.autoClicks);
009776:   const autoOrders = safeNum(row?.autoOrders);

009786:   // Must be truly承接ed by a manual campaign. If no manual spend/click trail exists, do not route Auto away.

009789:   if (!manualHasProof) return false;
009790: 
009791:   // P0 guardrail from real-account validation: do not negative Auto when Auto is more efficient.

010253:   const status = !economicsReady?"block":score >= minPass && orderGate ? "pass" : score >= minReview && (orders >= 1 || clicks >= 5) ? "review" : "block";

010255:   const bid = studioV3EstimateBid(row,bidMatch,context);
010256:   const reason = status === "pass"
010257:     ? getStudioText(`证据充分：${orders} 单 / ROAS ${roas.toFixed(2)} / 评分 ${score}`,`Strong evidence: ${orders} orders / ROAS ${roas.toFixed(2)} / score ${score}`)
010258:     : status === "review"
010259:       ? getStudioText(`有潜力但样本不足：${orders} 单 / ${orderDays || 0} 个出单日`,`Promising but limited sample: ${orders} orders / ${orderDays || 0} order days`)
010260:       : !economicsReady?getStudioText("缺少产品经济参数，禁止进入上线池","Missing product economics; launch is blocked"):getStudioText("证据或相关性不足，暂不进入上线池","Insufficient evidence or relevance; keep out of launch pool");
010261:   return { ...row, name, intentMeta:intent, studioScore:score, studioStatus:status, studioReason:reason, studioBid:bid.value, studioBidSource:bid.source, studioBidEstimated:bid.estimated, suggestedBid:row.suggestedBid || (bid.value ? bid.value.toFixed(2) : ""), studioEfficiency:efficiency, studioConfidence:confidence, studioProfitProxy:profitProxy, roas, cvr };

010316: const allocateStudioBudgetsV3 = (layers = [], data = {}) => {
010317:   const objectiveWeights = {

010319:     balanced:{AUTO_SEARCH:.08,AUTO_PRODUCT:.04,EXACT:.29,PHRASE:.19,BROAD:.05,PAT_ATTACK:.12,PAT_DEFENSE:.06,RANK_PUSH:.17},

010331:   });
010332:   const totalWeight = raw.reduce((s,x)=>s+x.weight,0) || 1;

010337:   const scale = data.totalBudget/sum;
010338:   const map = new Map(allocated.map(x=>[x.layer.key,Number((x.budget*scale).toFixed(2))]));
010339:   return layers.map(layer=>({ ...layer, dailyBudget:layer.key==="NEGATIVE"?0:(map.get(layer.key)||0), budgetShare:layer.key==="NEGATIVE"?0:(map.get(layer.key)||0)/Math.max(1,data.totalBudget) }));

012455: const sanitizeAIHtml = (inputHtml) => {
012456:     const template = document.createElement("template");
012457:     template.innerHTML = String(inputHtml || "").replace(/```html/g, "").replace(/```/g, "");
012458:     const allowedTags = new Set(["DIV","SPAN","P","BR","UL","OL","LI","STRONG","B","EM","I","CODE","H1","H2","H3","H4","TABLE","THEAD","TBODY","TR","TH","TD","BUTTON","CHART-CONFIG","CANVAS"]);
012459:     const allowedAttrs = new Set(["class","data-action","data-val","type","id","colspan","rowspan"]);
012460:     const allowedClasses = new Set(["tag","good","bad","warn","alert-banner","ai-trigger","ai-chart-container","small"]);
012461:     const walk = (node) => {
012462:         [...node.childNodes].forEach(child => {
012463:             if (child.nodeType === Node.COMMENT_NODE) { child.remove(); return; }
012464:             if (child.nodeType !== Node.ELEMENT_NODE) return;
012465:             const tag = child.tagName;
012466:             if (!allowedTags.has(tag)) {
012467:                 child.replaceWith(document.createTextNode(child.textContent || ""));
012468:                 return;
012469:             }
012470:             [...child.attributes].forEach(attr => {
012471:                 const name = attr.name.toLowerCase();
012472:                 if (name.startsWith("on") || !allowedAttrs.has(name)) { child.removeAttribute(attr.name); return; }
012473:                 if (name === "class") {
012474:                     const safe = attr.value.split(/\s+/).filter(c => allowedClasses.has(c)).join(" ");
012475:                     if (safe) child.setAttribute("class", safe); else child.removeAttribute("class");
012476:                 }
012477:                 if (name === "id" && !/^ai-chart-[a-z0-9]+$/i.test(attr.value)) child.removeAttribute("id");
012478:                 if (name === "type" && child.tagName === "BUTTON") child.setAttribute("type", "button");
012479:             });
012480:             if (tag === "BUTTON" && child.classList.contains("ai-trigger")) child.setAttribute("type", "button");
012481:             walk(child);
012482:         });
012483:     };
012484:     walk(template.content);
012485:     return template.innerHTML;
012486: };

012498:         
012499:         try {

013654:   const cleanSheetName=name=>String(name||'Sheet').slice(0,31).replace(/[\\/?*\[\]:]/g,'_')||'Sheet';
013655:   const normalizeCell=v=>{
013656:     if(v===null||v===undefined||v===''||(typeof v==='number'&&!Number.isFinite(v)))return '';
013657:     if(v instanceof Date)return v.toISOString();
013658:     if(typeof v==='object'){try{return JSON.stringify(v);}catch(e){return String(v);}}
013659:     return v;
013660:   };
013661:   const exportViaSheetJS=(sheets,filename)=>{
013662:     if(!window.XLSX?.utils?.book_new)return false;
013663:     const wb=window.XLSX.utils.book_new();
013664:     for(const s of sheets){
013665:       const aoa=[(s.headers||[]).map(normalizeCell),...(s.dataRows||[]).map(row=>(row||[]).map(normalizeCell))];
013666:       const ws=window.XLSX.utils.aoa_to_sheet(aoa);
013667:       if(aoa.length&&aoa[0].length){ws['!autofilter']={ref:window.XLSX.utils.encode_range({s:{r:0,c:0},e:{r:Math.max(0,aoa.length-1),c:aoa[0].length-1}})};ws['!freeze']={xSplit:0,ySplit:1};}
013668:       const widths=(s.headers||[]).map((h,i)=>{let max=String(h??'').length;for(const row of (s.dataRows||[]).slice(0,2000))max=Math.max(max,String(normalizeCell(row?.[i])).length);return{wch:Math.min(50,Math.max(10,max+2))};});
013669:       ws['!cols']=widths;
013670:       window.XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(wb,ws,cleanSheetName(s.sheetName));
013671:     }
013672:     window.XLSX.writeFile(wb,filename,{compression:true});
013673:     return true;
013674:   };
013675:   const exportViaExcelJS=async(sheets,filename)=>{
013676:     if(!window.ExcelJS?.Workbook)return false;
013677:     const wb=new window.ExcelJS.Workbook();wb.creator='Ads Operations Integrity OS';wb.created=new Date();
013678:     for(const s of sheets){
013679:       const ws=wb.addWorksheet(cleanSheetName(s.sheetName),{views:[{state:'frozen',ySplit:1}]});
013680:       const headers=(s.headers||[]).map(normalizeCell);const hr=ws.addRow(headers);hr.font={bold:true,color:{argb:'FFFFFFFF'}};hr.fill={type:'pattern',pattern:'solid',fgColor:{argb:'FF1F2937'}};hr.alignment={vertical:'middle'};
013681:       if(headers.length)ws.autoFilter={from:{row:1,column:1},to:{row:1,column:headers.length}};
013682:       for(const row of (s.dataRows||[]))ws.addRow((row||[]).map(normalizeCell));
013683:       ws.columns.forEach((col,i)=>{let max=String(headers[i]??'').length;col.eachCell({includeEmpty:false},cell=>{max=Math.max(max,String(cell.value??'').length);});col.width=Math.min(50,Math.max(10,max+2));});
013684:     }
013685:     const buffer=await wb.xlsx.writeBuffer();downloadBlob(new Blob([buffer],{type:'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.spreadsheetml.sheet'}),filename);return true;
013686:   };
013687:   const csvEscape=v=>{const s=String(normalizeCell(v));return /[",\n\r]/.test(s)?`"${s.replace(/"/g,'""')}"`:s;};
013688:   const exportCsvFallback=(sheets,filename)=>{

013690:     const csv='\uFEFF'+parts.join('\r\n');downloadBlob(new Blob([csv],{type:'text/csv;charset=utf-8'}),filename.replace(/\.xlsx$/i,'_fallback.csv'));
013691:   };
013692:   const exportFinanceWorkbook=async(sheets,filename)=>{

013694:     if(globalExporter){try{await globalExporter(sheets,filename);return'RICH_EXCEL';}catch(e){console.warn('Rich Excel export failed; falling back.',e);}}

014095: <script id="shopScopeUiV1">
014096: (() => {
014097:   'use strict';
014098:   const SHOPS = Object.freeze(['ALL','YTDBNS','YY','JJ']);
014099:   const SHOP_LABELS = Object.freeze({ALL:'全部店铺',YTDBNS:'YTDBNS 店铺',YY:'YY 店铺',JJ:'JJ 店铺'});
014100:   const STORAGE_KEY = 'lr_active_shop_scope';
014101:   const normalizeShop = value => {
014102:     const shop = String(value || '').trim().toUpperCase();
014103:     return SHOPS.includes(shop) ? shop : 'ALL';
014104:   };
014105:   const storage = {
014106:     get: () => { try { return localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY) || 'ALL'; } catch (_) { return 'ALL'; } },
014107:     set: value => { try { localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, value); } catch (_) {} }
014108:   };
014109:   let activeShop = normalizeShop(storage.get());
014110: 
014111:   const syncShopUi = shop => {
014112:     document.querySelectorAll('#privateCloudImportPanel [data-shop]').forEach(button => {
014113:       const selected = button.dataset.shop === shop;
014114:       button.classList.toggle('active', selected);
014115:       button.setAttribute('aria-pressed', selected ? 'true' : 'false');
014116:       button.setAttribute('aria-checked', selected ? 'true' : 'false');
014117:     });
014118:     const hint = document.getElementById('activeShopHint');
014119:     if (hint) hint.textContent = `当前：${shop} · ${SHOP_LABELS[shop]}`;
014120:     document.documentElement.dataset.activeShop = shop;
014121:   };
014122: 
014123:   const setActiveShop = (value, options = {}) => {
014124:     const next = normalizeShop(value);
014125:     const changed = next !== activeShop;
014126:     activeShop = next;
014127:     storage.set(next);
014128:     syncShopUi(next);
014129:     window.ACTIVE_SHOP = next;
014130:     if (changed || options.force) {
014131:       window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('lr:shop-change', {
014132:         detail: { shop: next, label: SHOP_LABELS[next], source: options.source || 'shop-selector' }
014133:       }));
014134:     }
014135:     if (!options.silent && changed) {
014136:       try {
014137:         if (typeof notify === 'function') notify(`分析店铺已切换为 ${next} · ${SHOP_LABELS[next]}`, 'good');
014138:       } catch (_) {}
014139:     }
014140:     return next;
014141:   };
014142: 
014143:   const mount = () => {
014144:     const panel = document.getElementById('privateCloudImportPanel');
014145:     const loadButton = document.getElementById('btnPrivateCloudImport');
014146:     const logoutButton = document.getElementById('btnPrivateCloudLogout');
014147:     const status = document.getElementById('privateCloudImportStatus');
014148:     if (!panel || !loadButton || !logoutButton || !status) return false;
014149:     if (panel.dataset.shopUiReady === '1') {
014150:       syncShopUi(activeShop);
014151:       return true;
014152:     }
014153: 
014154:     loadButton.textContent = '☁ 加载私有云数据';
014155:     logoutButton.textContent = '清除密码';
014156:     const shell = document.createElement('div');
014157:     shell.innerHTML = `
014158:       <div class="cloudPanelHeader">
014159:         <div class="cloudPanelIcon" aria-hidden="true">☁</div>
014160:         <div class="cloudPanelCopy">
014161:           <div class="cloudPanelTitle">私有云数据</div>
014162:           <div class="cloudPanelSub">选择分析店铺，再安全读取广告、交易与成本数据</div>
014163:         </div>
014164:         <span class="cloudProviderBadge">CLOUDFLARE</span>
014165:       </div>
014166:       <div class="shopScopeCard">
014167:         <div class="shopScopeHead">
014168:           <span class="shopScopeLabel">店铺范围</span>
014169:           <span id="activeShopHint"></span>
014170:         </div>
014171:         <div class="shopScopeSwitch" role="radiogroup" aria-label="分析店铺范围">
014172:           ${SHOPS.map(shop => `<button class="shopScopeButton" type="button" role="radio" data-shop="${shop}" aria-label="${SHOP_LABELS[shop]}">${shop}</button>`).join('')}
014173:         </div>
014174:       </div>
014175:       <div class="privateCloudActions">
014176:         <span data-slot="load"></span>
014177:         <span data-slot="logout"></span>
014178:       </div>
014179:       <div class="cloudStatusRow">
014180:         <span class="cloudStatusDot" aria-hidden="true"></span>
014181:         <span data-slot="status"></span>
014182:       </div>`;
014183: 
014184:     shell.querySelector('[data-slot="load"]').replaceWith(loadButton);
014185:     shell.querySelector('[data-slot="logout"]').replaceWith(logoutButton);
014186:     shell.querySelector('[data-slot="status"]').replaceWith(status);
014187:     panel.replaceChildren(...shell.childNodes);
014188:     panel.dataset.shopUiReady = '1';
014189:     panel.addEventListener('click', event => {
014190:       const button = event.target.closest('[data-shop]');
014191:       if (!button || !panel.contains(button)) return;
014192:       setActiveShop(button.dataset.shop, { source: 'data-import-panel' });
014193:     });
014194:     setActiveShop(activeShop, { silent: true, force: true, source: 'initialization' });
014195:     return true;
014196:   };
014197: 
014198:   const init = () => {
014199:     let attempts = 0;
014200:     const tryMount = () => {
014201:       if (mount()) return;
014202:       attempts += 1;
014203:       if (attempts < 120) requestAnimationFrame(tryMount);
014204:     };
014205:     tryMount();
014206:     window.ShopScope = Object.freeze({
014207:       options: SHOPS,
014208:       labels: SHOP_LABELS,
014209:       get: () => activeShop,
014210:       set: value => setActiveShop(value, { source: 'api' })
014211:     });
014212:   };
014213: 
014214:   if (document.readyState === 'loading') document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init, { once: true });
014215:   else init();
014216: })();
014217: </script>
